References</h3><ul><li><strong>major treatment</strong><ul><li><div class="md-assembly-wrapper" data-type="image"><div class="image-wrapper "><img src="https://cdn.britannica.com/190x500/43/3843-004-E9DA70FA.jpg" big-src="https://cdn.britannica.com/43/3843-004-E9DA70FA.jpg" alt="Russia" data-width="606" data-height="435"></div></div> <span class="index-xref">In <a href="https://www.britannica.com/place/Russia/History#ref421617" class="md-crosslink">Russia: Prehistory and the rise of the Rus</a></span><p>…is now the territory of Russia since the 2nd millennium <span class="text-smallcaps">bce</span>, but little is known about their ethnic identity, institutions, and activities. In ancient times, Greek and Iranian settlements appeared in the southernmost portions of what is now Ukraine.
